The Language of Gbempöktöian

Natively known as: Gbempöktö /gbɛmˈpəktə/

...and he stood holding his hat and turned his wet face to the wind...
ti ngi put hōd fot fok ti umpekpom o put wom wöf rim
Pronunciation: /ti ŋi put hoːd fɔt fɔk ti umˈpɛkpɔm ɔ put wɔm wəf rim/
Gbempöktöian word order: and he his hat holding stood and the wind to his wet face turned

Spelling & Phonology

Consonant inventory: /b d f g gb h k kp l m p r s t w x ŋ ʃ ʔ/

↓Manner/Place→ BilabialLabiodentalAlveolarPalato-alveolarVelarLabio-velarGlottal

Vowel inventory: /eː i oː u ɑ ɔ ə ɛ ɪ ʊ/

Syllable structure: (C)V(C)
Stress pattern: No fixed stress
Word initial consonants: b, d, f, g, gb, h, k, kp, l, m, p, r, s, t, w, x, ŋ, ʃ, ʔ
Mid-word consonants: b, bd, d, f, g, gm, gb, h, k, kp, ks, kt, kp, l, lk, m, mb, mp, p, pl, r, rk, rm, rs, rx, s, sp, st, t, w, x, ŋ, ŋh, ʃ, ʔ
Word final consonants: b, d, f, g, gb, k, kp, l, m, r, s, t, w, x, ŋ

Phonological rules (in order of application):

  • l → ɾ / V_V
  • s → t / _#
  • s → h / _#
  • {p,k} → [+voice] / V_V
Spelling rules:

Grammar

Main word order: Subject-Oblique-Object-Verb. "Mary opened the door with a key" turns into Mary with a key the door opened.
Adjective order: Adjectives are positioned before the noun.
Adposition: postpositions

Noun

Nouns form plural with separate plural word:

Plural mo /mɔ/
plural particle

Nouns have four cases:
Ergative is the doer of a verb: dog bites man
The ergative affix only appears if there is an absolutive in the sentence
Absolutive is the done-to of a verb: man bites dog
Absolutives are always no affix
Genitive is the possessor of something: dog’s tail hits man
Dative is the recipeint of something: man gives ball to dog

Masculine Feminine Neuter
Ergative If ends with vowel: Suffix -x
Else: Suffix -ix

Articles

Gbempöktöian has no definite article ‘the’, or indefinite article ‘a’.

Verbs

Present No affix
ngumö /ˈŋumə/

Else: Suffix -oːfi
ngumöfi /ŋuˈməfi/

Imperfective aspect

The ‘imperfective’ aspect refers to ongoing actions, such as I am studying,
and habitual actions, such as I study (every night).

It is indicated with the word:

Imperfect particle kpo /kpɔ/
imperfect particle

Derivational morphology

Adjective → noun = Suffix -um
Noun → adjective = If ends with vowel: Suffix -sɑ
Else: Suffix -ʊsɑ
Noun → verb = Suffix -ʊ
Verb → noun = Suffix -oːb
Verb → adjective = If ends with vowel: Suffix -g
Else: Suffix -ʊg
Adjective → verb = Suffix -ɛr
Adjective → adverb = Suffix -əd
One who Xs (e.g. paint → painter) = Suffix -il
Place of (e.g. wine → winery) = Suffix -ʊg
Diminutive = Suffix -ɑkp
Augmentative = Suffix -ɛkp
